**GT:** `-0.0586*v³ - 0.7167*v - 0.3583*v*exp(-|v|) + 0.6686*sin(t)`

Note that `sin(t) = cos(t - π/2) = cos(-π/2 + t)`, so `cos(c + t)` with appropriate c can represent `sin(t)`.

The GT has these terms:
1. A `v` term (linear in v)
2. A `v³` term
3. A `sin(t)` term (equivalently `cos(c + t)`)
4. A `v*exp(-|v|)` term

The key challenge is matching the `v*exp(-|v|)` term. Let me check which candidates could produce this.

**Candidates with `v*exp(...)` terms:** 8, 16, 17, 24, 25, 38, 42, 57

**Candidate 17:** `c0*v + c1*cos(c2 + t) + c3*v*exp(c4*v²) + c5*v*exp(c6*|v|)`

Wait - could `c3*v*exp(c4*v²)` approximate `v³`? No, we need exact equivalence.

This matches the GT structure exactly:
- c0 = -0.7167 (for the v term)

- c7 = -0.3583 (for v*exp(-|v|))

**Candidate 16 matches!**
